<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">SignaturePad.Control</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">SignaturePad.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="image-preview" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#image-preview"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Image Preview</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">After the user draws a signature, you can display a preview of the signature as an image. This is useful when you want
to show the user a preview of the signature before saving it.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="field" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#field"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Field</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Field</code> component helps manage form-related state and accessibility attributes of a signature pad. It includes
handling ARIA labels, helper text, and error text to ensure proper accessibility.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the signature pad is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useSignaturePad</code> hook.
This way you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>

<h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">API</h3><div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto my_8 not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm This is useful when you want\nto show the user a preview of the signature before saving it.\n\n**Example: image-preview**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { SignaturePad } from '@ark-ui/react/signature-pad'\nimport { RotateCcwIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/signature-pad.module.css'\n\nexport const ImagePreview = () =\u003e {\n  const [imageUrl, setImageUrl] = useState('')\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cSignaturePad.Root\n        className={styles.Root}\n        onDrawEnd={(details) =\u003e details.getDataUrl('image/png').then((url) =\u003e setImageUrl(url))}\n      \u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eSign below\u003c/SignaturePad.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cSignaturePad.Segment className={styles.Segment} /\u003e\n          \u003cSignaturePad.ClearTrigger className={styles.ClearTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cRotateCcwIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/SignaturePad.ClearTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cSignaturePad.Guide className={styles.Guide} /\u003e\n        \u003c/SignaturePad.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/SignaturePad.Root\u003e\n\n      \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n        \u003cspan\u003eImage Preview\u003c/span\u003e\n        {imageUrl \u0026\u0026 \u003cimg src={imageUrl} alt=\"Signature\" className={styles.Image} /\u003e}\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { SignaturePad } from '@ark-ui/solid/signature-pad'\nimport { RotateCcwIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Show, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/signature-pad.module.css'\n\nexport const ImagePreview = () =\u003e {\n  const [imageUrl, setImageUrl] = createSignal('')\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cSignaturePad.Root\n        class={styles.Root}\n        onDrawEnd={(details) =\u003e details.getDataUrl('image/png').then((url) =\u003e setImageUrl(url))}\n      \u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eSign below\u003c/SignaturePad.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cSignaturePad.Segment class={styles.Segment} /\u003e\n          \u003cSignaturePad.ClearTrigger class={styles.ClearTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cRotateCcwIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/SignaturePad.ClearTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cSignaturePad.Guide class={styles.Guide} /\u003e\n        \u003c/SignaturePad.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/SignaturePad.Root\u003e\n\n      \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n        \u003cspan\u003eImage Preview\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cShow when={imageUrl()}\u003e\n          \u003cimg src={imageUrl()} alt=\"Signature\" class={styles.Image} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Show\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { SignaturePad, type SignaturePadDrawEndDetails } from '@ark-ui/vue/signature-pad'\nimport { RotateCcwIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/signature-pad.module.css'\n\nconst imageUrl = ref('')\n\nconst handleDrawEnd = async (details: SignaturePadDrawEndDetails) =\u003e {\n  imageUrl.value = await details.getDataUrl('image/png')\n}\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003cSignaturePad.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" @draw-end=\"handleDrawEnd\"\u003e\n      \u003cSignaturePad.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eSign below\u003c/SignaturePad.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSignaturePad.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.Segment :class=\"styles.Segment\" /\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.ClearTrigger :class=\"styles.ClearTrigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cRotateCcwIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/SignaturePad.ClearTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.Guide :class=\"styles.Guide\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/SignaturePad.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/SignaturePad.Root\u003e\n\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cspan\u003eImage Preview\u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003cimg v-if=\"imageUrl\" :src=\"imageUrl\" alt=\"Signature\" :class=\"styles.Image\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { SignaturePad } from '@ark-ui/svelte/signature-pad'\n  import RotateCcwIcon from 'lucide-svelte/icons/rotate-ccw'\n  import styles from 'styles/signature-pad.module.css'\n\n  let imageUrl = $state('')\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003cSignaturePad.Root\n    class={styles.Root}\n    onDrawEnd={(details) =\u003e details.getDataUrl('image/png').then((url) =\u003e (imageUrl = url))}\n  \u003e\n    \u003cSignaturePad.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eSign below\u003c/SignaturePad.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSignaturePad.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cSignaturePad.Segment class={styles.Segment} /\u003e\n      \u003cSignaturePad.ClearTrigger class={styles.ClearTrigger}\u003e\n        \u003cRotateCcwIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/SignaturePad.ClearTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cSignaturePad.Guide class={styles.Guide} /\u003e\n    \u003c/SignaturePad.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/SignaturePad.Root\u003e\n\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003cspan\u003eImage Preview\u003c/span\u003e\n    {#if imageUrl}\n      \u003cimg src={imageUrl} alt=\"Signature\" class={styles.Image} /\u003e\n    {/if}\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Field\n\nThe `Field` component helps manage form-related state and accessibility attributes of a signature pad. It includes\nhandling ARIA labels, helper text, and error text to ensure proper accessibility.\n\n**Example: with-field**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/react/field'\nimport { SignaturePad } from '@ark-ui/react/signature-pad'\nimport { RotateCcwIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/signature-pad.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cField.Root className={field.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cSignaturePad.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cSignaturePad.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/SignaturePad.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSignaturePad.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.Segment className={styles.Segment} /\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.ClearTrigger className={styles.ClearTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cRotateCcwIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/SignaturePad.ClearTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.Guide className={styles.Guide} /\u003e\n      \u003c/SignaturePad.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/SignaturePad.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText className={field.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText className={field.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/solid/field'\nimport { SignaturePad } from '@ark-ui/solid/signature-pad'\nimport { RotateCcwIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/signature-pad.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cSignaturePad.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cSignaturePad.Label  \u003cSignaturePad.ClearTrigger class={styles.ClearTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cRotateCcwIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/SignaturePad.ClearTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.Guide Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/vue/field'\nimport { SignaturePad } from '@ark-ui/vue/signature-pad'\nimport { RotateCcwIcon } from Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n\u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the signature pad is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useSignaturePad` hook.\nThis way you can access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { SignaturePad, useSignaturePad } from '@ark-ui/react/signature-pad'\nimport { RotateCcwIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/signature-pad.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const signaturePad = useSignaturePad()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003eno of paths: {signaturePad.paths.length}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cSignaturePad.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={signaturePad}\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eSign below\u003c/SignaturePad.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cSignaturePad.Segment className={styles.Segment} /\u003e\n          \u003cSignaturePad.ClearTrigger className={styles.ClearTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cRotateCcwIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/SignaturePad.ClearTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cSignaturePad.Guide className={styles.Guide} /\u003e\n        \u003c/SignaturePad.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/SignaturePad.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { SignaturePad, useSignaturePad } from '@ark-ui/solid/signature-pad'\nimport { RotateCcwIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/signature-pad.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const signaturePad = useSignaturePad()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003eno of paths: {signaturePad().paths.length}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cSignaturePad.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={signaturePad}\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eSign below\u003c/SignaturePad.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cSignaturePad.Segment class={styles.Segment} /\u003e\n          \u003cSignaturePad.ClearTrigger class={styles.ClearTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cRotateCcwIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/SignaturePad.ClearTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cSignaturePad.Guide class={styles.Guide} /\u003e\n        \u003c/SignaturePad.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/SignaturePad.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { SignaturePad, useSignaturePad } from '@ark-ui/vue/signature-pad'\nimport { RotateCcwIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/signature-pad.module.css'\n\nconst signaturePad = useSignaturePad()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003coutput\u003eno of paths: {{ signaturePad.paths.length }}\u003c/output\u003e\n    \u003cSignaturePad.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"signaturePad\"\u003e\n      \u003cSignaturePad.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eSign below\u003c/SignaturePad.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSignaturePad.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.Segment :class=\"styles.Segment\" /\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.ClearTrigger :class=\"styles.ClearTrigger\"\u003e\n          \u003cRotateCcwIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/SignaturePad.ClearTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cSignaturePad.Guide :class=\"styles.Guide\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/SignaturePad.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/SignaturePad.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n####
